=begin
= Serif setting for skill (for enemy)

    :word_1  ...Serif information. Contents, name of facial ware file, headquarters index order.
                :word_1From:word_10We decide randomly from among.
    :ct_type ...Specify the cut-in type from the following. (Currently 4 types)
      :basic ... Simple display
      :slide ... Slide in from the right
      :focus ... Gather at the origin with 3 layers display
      :long  ... Simple display without effect sound. It remains until the damage is over
    :ct_pic  ...Picture name to be displayed in cut-in
    :ct_se   ...SE name to play when cut in
    
For the cut-in type, because the display origin is changed
I can not do as I have done so far so I will add it appropriately.


==Change log
Date     Version Author Comment

=end
